# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Envoy Stats Scope and Tag Architecture

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in envoyproxy/envoy that implement the stats system: the Stats::Scope hierarchy, the tag extraction from metric names, the stat name interning (StatNamePool), and the stat sink dispatch for Prometheus and statsd output.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2, sg-evals/data-plane-api--84e84367, sg-evals/go-control-plane--71637ad6, sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2` (envoyproxy/envoy)

- `sg-evals/grpc--957dba5e` (grpc/grpc)

I've created `/workspace/answer.json` containing:

**57 C++ source files** across these key areas:

1. **Core Stats Interfaces** (15 files in `envoy/stats/`): Define Scope hierarchy, Store management, Sink dispatch, Tag extraction, and metric types

2. **Stats Implementations** (27 files in `source/common/stats/`): 
   - Thread-local and isolated store implementations
   - StatNamePool and symbol table for stat name interning
   - Tag producer and extractor implementations for extracting tags from metric names
   - Metric implementations (counters, gauges, histograms, text readouts)

3. **Stat Sinks** (14 files across `source/extensions/stat_sinks/`):
   - **StatsD family**: UDP/TCP statsd with tag format support (Datadog, InfluxDB, Graphite)
   - **Hystrix**: Dashboard-compatible real-time metrics
   - **gRPC Metrics Service**: Remote metrics collection via gRPC
   - **OpenTelemetry**: Modern observability platform integration
   - **Wasm**: WebAssembly-extensible sink implementations

4. **Prometheus Output** (2 files): Admin endpoint for Prometheus text format metrics

The narrative explanation details the complete architecture including the Scope hierarchy, tag extraction pipeline, stat name interning mechanism, thread-local store with fast-path caching, and the sink dispatch system that routes metrics to external systems.

\"source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.cc\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Envoy stats system is organized into several key components implemented across the v1.31.2 codebase:\\n\\n## Core Stats Hierarchy (envoy/stats/)\\n\\nThe foundational interfaces are defined in envoy/stats/. The Stats::Scope hierarchy is defined in scope.h, representing scoped statistics that inherit from parent scopes. The Store interface (store.h) manages all scopes and provides access to the root scope. The Allocator interface (allocator.h) is responsible for creating new stat metrics.\\n\\n## Stat Name Interning (StatNamePool)\\n\\nStatistic names are interned through the SymbolTable mechanism (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h and symbol_table.cc). The StatNamePool class provides pooled allocation and management of StatName objects for efficient memory reuse. This is a critical optimization for handling high-cardinality metric names without excessive memory consumption.\\n\\n## Tag Extraction Architecture\\n\\nTags are extracted from metric names through a two-level system:\\n- TagExtractor interface and implementations (envoy/stats/tag_extractor.h, source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h/cc): Provides regex-based and fixed-value tag extraction patterns\\n- TagProducer interface and implementation (envoy/stats/tag_producer.h, source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h/cc): Coordinates multiple extractors to extract all tags from a metric name\\n- TagUtility (source/common/stats/tag_utility.h/cc): Helper functions for tag operations and StatName construction with tags\\n\\n## Thread-Local Store Implementation\\n\\nThe thread-safe, high-performance stats store is implemented in source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h/cc. The ThreadLocalStoreImpl::ScopeImpl class manages per-scope metrics and provides methods like counterFromStatNameWithTags, gaugeFromStatNameWithTags, and histogramFromStatNameWithTags. The implementation includes thread-local caching and proper scope hierarchy management.\\n\\n## Alternative Store Implementations\\n\\nThe IsolatedStoreImpl (source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h/cc) provides a non-thread-safe implementation useful for testing and isolated stat collections. Both implementations support the common Store interface for polymorphism.\\n\\n## Metric Implementation\\n\\nIndividual metric types are implemented in:\\n- histogram_impl.h/cc: Counter, gauge, and histogram metric implementations including thread-local histograms (ThreadLocalHistogramImpl) and parent histograms (ParentHistogramImpl)\\n- metric_impl.h/cc: Base MetricHelper class providing common metric functionality\\n- Null implementations (null_counter.h, null_gauge.h, null_text_readout.h): No-op metrics for disabled stats\\n\\n## Sink Architecture and Dispatch\\n\\nThe Sink interface (envoy/stats/sink.h) defines how stats are flushed to external systems. The dispatch mechanism is implemented in the Store, which maintains a list of sinks and calls onStaticCountersIterator, onHistogramComplete, etc. on each sink.\\n\\n## Stat Sink Implementations\\n\\nMultiple sink implementations handle different output formats:\\n\\n1. **StatsD/Metrics Service (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/)**: \\n   - UdpStatsdSink and TcpStatsdSink implement statsd protocol output\\n   - tag_formats.h/cc handles different tagging conventions (Datadog, InfluxDB, etc.)\\n\\n2. **Statsd Factory (source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/)**: config.h/cc registers the statsd sink factory\\n\\n3. **DogStatsd (source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/)**: Datadog-compatible statsd sink factory\\n\\n4. **GraphiteStatsd (source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/)**: Graphite-compatible statsd sink factory\\n\\n5. **Hystrix (source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/)**: \\n   - hystrix.h/cc implements the Hystrix dashboard compatible sink\\n   - Provides real-time metrics for Hystrix circuit breaker visualization\\n\\n6. **gRPC Metrics Service (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/)**: \\n   - grpc_metrics_service_impl.h/cc implements templated MetricsServiceSink\\n   - Supports flushing to external metrics services via gRPC\\n   - grpc_metrics_proto_descriptors.h/cc provides proto definitions\\n\\n7. **OpenTelemetry (source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/)**: \\n   - open_telemetry_impl.h/cc provides OpenTelemetry-compatible metrics export\\n   - Supports OTLP protocol for modern observability platforms\\n\\n8. **Wasm (source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/)**: \\n   - wasm_stat_sink_impl.h enables stats sinks written in WebAssembly\\n   - Allows extensible sink implementations without core changes\\n\\n## Prometheus Output\\n\\nThe Prometheus stats formatter (source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.h/cc) converts Envoy stats to Prometheus text format for the /stats/prometheus admin endpoint. This uses the tag extraction system to properly format Prometheus labels.\\n\\n## Supporting Systems\\n\\n- **StatsMatcherImpl (stats_matcher_impl.h/cc)**: Implements stat filtering based on inclusion/exclusion patterns\\n- **Allocator Implementation (allocator_impl.h/cc)**: Manages memory allocation and lifecycle for metric objects\\n- **StatMerger (stat_merger.h/cc)**: Merges stats from multiple Envoy processes (used in hot restart)\\n- **Deferred Creation (deferred_creation.h)**: Supports lazy initialization of stats structures\\n\\nThe architecture ensures lock-free fast-path access on per-thread caches while maintaining global stat consistency through proper synchronization on the slow path.\"\n}\n",

\"source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.cc\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Envoy stats system is organized into several key components implemented across the v1.31.2 codebase:\\n\\n## Core Stats Hierarchy (envoy/stats/)\\n\\nThe foundational interfaces are defined in envoy/stats/. The Stats::Scope hierarchy is defined in scope.h, representing scoped statistics that inherit from parent scopes. The Store interface (store.h) manages all scopes and provides access to the root scope. The Allocator interface (allocator.h) is responsible for creating new stat metrics.\\n\\n## Stat Name Interning (StatNamePool)\\n\\nStatistic names are interned through the SymbolTable mechanism (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h and symbol_table.cc). The StatNamePool class provides pooled allocation and management of StatName objects for efficient memory reuse. This is a critical optimization for handling high-cardinality metric names without excessive memory consumption.\\n\\n## Tag Extraction Architecture\\n\\nTags are extracted from metric names through a two-level system:\\n- TagExtractor interface and implementations (envoy/stats/tag_extractor.h, source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h/cc): Provides regex-based and fixed-value tag extraction patterns\\n- TagProducer interface and implementation (envoy/stats/tag_producer.h, source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h/cc): Coordinates multiple extractors to extract all tags from a metric name\\n- TagUtility (source/common/stats/tag_utility.h/cc): Helper functions for tag operations and StatName construction with tags\\n\\n## Thread-Local Store Implementation\\n\\nThe thread-safe, high-performance stats store is implemented in source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h/cc. The ThreadLocalStoreImpl::ScopeImpl class manages per-scope metrics and provides methods like counterFromStatNameWithTags, gaugeFromStatNameWithTags, and histogramFromStatNameWithTags. The implementation includes thread-local caching and proper scope hierarchy management.\\n\\n## Alternative Store Implementations\\n\\nThe IsolatedStoreImpl (source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h/cc) provides a non-thread-safe implementation useful for testing and isolated stat collections. Both implementations support the common Store interface for polymorphism.\\n\\n## Metric Implementation\\n\\nIndividual metric types are implemented in:\\n- histogram_impl.h/cc: Counter, gauge, and histogram metric implementations including thread-local histograms (ThreadLocalHistogramImpl) and parent histograms (ParentHistogramImpl)\\n- metric_impl.h/cc: Base MetricHelper class providing common metric functionality\\n- Null implementations (null_counter.h, null_gauge.h, null_text_readout.h): No-op metrics for disabled stats\\n\\n## Sink Architecture and Dispatch\\n\\nThe Sink interface (envoy/stats/sink.h) defines how stats are flushed to external systems. The dispatch mechanism is implemented in the Store, which maintains a list of sinks and calls onStaticCountersIterator, onHistogramComplete, etc. on each sink.\\n\\n## Stat Sink Implementations\\n\\nMultiple sink implementations handle different output formats:\\n\\n1. **StatsD/Metrics Service (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/)**: \\n   - UdpStatsdSink and TcpStatsdSink implement statsd protocol output\\n   - tag_formats.h/cc handles different tagging conventions (Datadog, InfluxDB, etc.)\\n\\n2. **Statsd Factory (source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/)**: config.h/cc registers the statsd sink factory\\n\\n3. **DogStatsd (source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/)**: Datadog-compatible statsd sink factory\\n\\n4. **GraphiteStatsd (source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/)**: Graphite-compatible statsd sink factory\\n\\n5. **Hystrix (source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/)**: \\n   - hystrix.h/cc implements the Hystrix dashboard compatible sink\\n   - Provides real-time metrics for Hystrix circuit breaker visualization\\n\\n6. **gRPC Metrics Service (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/)**: \\n   - grpc_metrics_service_impl.h/cc implements templated MetricsServiceSink\\n   - Supports flushing to external metrics services via gRPC\\n   - grpc_metrics_proto_descriptors.h/cc provides proto definitions\\n\\n7. **OpenTelemetry (source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/)**: \\n   - open_telemetry_impl.h/cc provides OpenTelemetry-compatible metrics export\\n   - Supports OTLP protocol for modern observability platforms\\n\\n8. **Wasm (source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/)**: \\n   - wasm_stat_sink_impl.h enables stats sinks written in WebAssembly\\n   - Allows extensible sink implementations without core changes\\n\\n## Prometheus Output\\n\\nThe Prometheus stats formatter (source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.h/cc) converts Envoy stats to Prometheus text format for the /stats/prometheus admin endpoint. This uses the tag extraction system to properly format Prometheus labels.\\n\\n## Supporting Systems\\n\\n- **StatsMatcherImpl (stats_matcher_impl.h/cc)**: Implements stat filtering based on inclusion/exclusion patterns\\n- **Allocator Implementation (allocator_impl.h/cc)**: Manages memory allocation and lifecycle for metric objects\\n- **StatMerger (stat_merger.h/cc)**: Merges stats from multiple Envoy processes (used in hot restart)\\n- **Deferred Creation (deferred_creation.h)**: Supports lazy initialization of stats structures\\n\\nThe architecture ensures lock-free fast-path access on per-thread caches while maintaining global stat consistency through proper synchronization on the slow path.\"\n}\n",
